[30;1m3 | [0m[35m======[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35mTooz provides distributed locks. A lock is identified by a name, and a lock can[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35monly be acquired by one coordinator at a time.[0m

[30;1m6 | [0m[35mobjects (represented via binary keys) to one or several nodes. When the node[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mlist changes, the rebalancing of objects across the ring is kept minimal.[0m
